msg:The first check-in on 2023-12-18 was a good experience. Although there were some minor flaws in the service box details, the staff actively dealt with it at the time, so although many details were not satisfactory, it was understandable.

I checked in again on 2024-02-27. I was still looking forward to it before checking in. After all, it is a five-star hotel under InterContinental. I thought it would not be checked, but this time the good impression was gone.
First of all, the front desk service. I booked two rooms, one for check-in first and the other for check-in later. The staff who handled it did not hand over well. After I checked in first and paid a deposit of 2,000 yuan, they asked my family to charge 1,200 yuan to ensure that there was consumption? ! My family was confused at the time, but it was more than seven o'clock when they arrived. My family drove for more than an hour, so they went to the 3rd floor Yugongguan for dinner first. They didn't ask much and paid first. After the meal, I needed to take my ID card and go downstairs again to wait for the front desk to verify again, and then the front desk returned more than 1,000 yuan. We raised our doubts, and the front desk said that the colleague who handled it before did not hand over clearly. Should such a complicated procedure exist in a hotel of this level? Does the check-in verification and confirmation procedure need to be optimized? Should every front desk receptionist be proficient in it?

In addition, I booked two rooms. Even if we did not check in at the same time, when I checked in first, should the reception staff take the initiative to ask whether it was a family trip? Do we need to arrange the same floor? I think the front desk receptionist should have this kind of forward-looking service awareness. So when my family checked in at night, they wanted to stay on the same floor, but the room type required by the front desk staff could not be arranged, so my family and I had one room on the 10th floor and one room on the 17th floor.

Secondly, in a five-star hotel, the mini bar was empty? Regarding welcome fruit, we had prepared welcome fruit when we checked in before, and we also booked through Ctrip. So this time we wondered why there was no preparation, so at the request of my family, we finally changed from denying the welcome fruit to replying that we could prepare it. But the banana that was delivered was like the picture. If the welcome fruit you prepared looked like this, then I really couldn't figure out whether the hotel was welcoming or not? ? ! ! Besides, this fruit is not necessary to eat, it just requires an attitude! !

Finally, I have to complain about the breakfast buffet, which is much different from the previous ones. There are fewer varieties, and the taste and texture of the dishes have also deteriorated. The Chinese pancakes used to be taro pancakes, which had a very good texture and taste. This time, they were replaced with radish cakes, which were not delicious at all. They were all powdery, without any radish taste... The soup noodles had no taste at all, and the meatballs with them also had a very bad taste. Funny thing, there was no tray? When we took the soup noodles, we could only hold the bowl directly. The hot and spicy soup noodles that were just cooked, even if you think not everyone needs them, you should prepare a certain amount for backup, right? The fried red sausages, the beef balls with boiled noodles, and the cuttlefish balls had a heavy powdery taste when you bite them, and they were not delicious at all. After all, it is a five-star hotel. Why don‚Äôt you choose better manufacturers and brands for ingredients that can be purchased all over the street? The beans in tomato sauce are not hot... The speed and temperature of the food should be paid attention to and improved in time. What's even funnier is that during breakfast, there were actually a lot of managers in suits walking around in the restaurant. They all looked very busy, but I didn't know what they were busy with... Because even though the restaurant had more people, they didn't take the initiative to check if the guests had any other needs or guide the guests entering the restaurant. Several people were just looking at their phones or walking around. There were so many people that it was a bit inexplicable.
Although it is a newly opened hotel, this is not a reason for poor service. I hope the hotel can pay attention and improve its service.

msg:During the National Day, we stayed at the newly opened Jiangmen Crowne Plaza Hotel. Let‚Äôs talk about the external environment first. The surrounding area is under construction, there are no shops or restaurants, and the sound of pile drivers at the construction site can be heard. As for the internal environment, the room basically does not have the decoration smell of a new house. But when I opened the wooden cabinet, there was still the smell of new furniture. In the room I stayed in, the toilet was built in the center of the room, surrounded by the bed and sink. And if you open the toilet door, even if the toilet is clean, there will still be a strong and pungent smell of sewer filling the room. In terms of service, first of all, on the day of arrival, check-in was clearly available at 14:00, but we did not get the room until 18:40, and the executive lounge was not open. We could only rest and wait in the air-conditioned lobby bar. The so-called happy hour set menu is also weird. The menu is not printed and I don't know what it is. The details are not enough, and the administrative courtesy service needs to be strengthened. Due to the large number of people, the breakfast service was moved to the conference room. There are quite a lot of varieties, but there is no vinaigrette on the side of the salad? Then the waiter took away the finished plates but did not take away the used napkins. It can be seen that most of the waiters are new, and they started working just in time for the National Day opening without adequate training. It took a long time for room service to respond after calling, obviously understaffed. One day, on the sofa facing the front desk, a lady was preparing to check in with her pet dog, taking crazy selfies. It was so conspicuous that no one at the front desk noticed. It was only after I reminded him verbally that the front desk found out. If she is allowed to bring a pet in, the floor of the room is covered with carpets, and the dog urinates in it, and the housekeeping lady will only work hard to clean it, and then any guest will stay in the room where the pet dog once lived. If allergies occur, it is also very unfair to other guests. Is it possible to place a reminder that pets are not allowed in a prominent location? During my stay, all the service staff I met had very good attitudes and worked very hard to satisfy customers. They are just relatively inexperienced and relatively new. The National Day in 2023 is said to have the highest number of tourists in history. Maybe it is a bit overwhelmed when a newly opened hotel faces such a large passenger flow. As a long-term senior member of InterContinental, I also express my understanding and tolerance. Hope to do better and better.
